id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><h1><span id="ctl00_ctl00_uxMainContent_uxMainContent_lblTitle">Ruger Precision Rifle, Bolt Action, .243 Win, 26", Folding Stock, Black</span></h1> <p>Scope not included</p><p> </p><h3>Purpose-built to distance itself from the typical long-range rifle.</h3> <p>The&nbsp;<a href="http://ruger.com/micros/rpr/index.html" target="_blank">Ruger Precision Rifle</a>&nbsp;is a highly configurable, in-line recoil path, bolt-action rifle.&nbsp;</p> <p>Features</p> <h3>Features</h3> <li><font>Medium contour (.75' at the muzzle) barrel features 5/8'-24 threads. Thread protector installed.</font></li> <li><font>Barrels can be easily replaced by a competent gunsmith using AR-style wrenches and headspace gauges.</font></li> <li><font>Highly accurate Ruger cold hammer-forged&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/41xx_steel" target="_blank">4140 chrome-moly steel</a>&nbsp;barrel with 5R Rifling at minimum bore and groove dimensions, minimum headspace and centralized chamber.</font></li> <li><font>Equipped with a Samson Evolution Keymod Handguard. May be configured with any AR-style handguard.</font></li> <li><font>Magazine well front is contoured for a positive grip for bracing against shooting supports.</font></li> <li><font>20 MOA&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Picatinny_rail" target="_blank">Picatinny rail</a>&nbsp;secured with four, #8-40 screws for increased long-range elevation capabilities.</font></li> <li><font>'Lower' magazine well halves are precision machined from aerospace-grade&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/7075_aluminium_alloy" target="_blank">7075-T6 aluminum</a>&nbsp;forging and are Type III hard coat anodized for maximum durability.</font></li> <li><font>'Upper' receiver and one-piece bolt are precision CNC-machined from pre-hardened 4140 chrome-moly steel to minimize distortion.</font></li> <li><font>Multi-Magazine Interface functions interchangeably with M110, SR25, DPMS and Magpul-style magazines and AICS magazines (works with some M-14 magazines); two 10-round Magpul PMAG magazines included.</font></li> <li><font>Three-lug bolt with 70 throw features dual cocking cams and a smooth-running, full diameter bolt body.</font></li> <li><font>Ruger Marksman Adjustable trigger is externally adjustable with a pull weight range of 2.25 to 5.0 lbs.; wrench is stored in the bolt shroud.</font></li> <li><font>Oversized bolt handle for positive bolt manipulation, with 5/16'-24 thread for easy replacement. Bolt disassembly tool is stored in the bolt shroud for easy striker channel cleaning.</font></li> <li><font>In-line recoil path manages recoil directly from the rear of the receiver to the buttstock, not through a traditional bedding system, providing maximum accuracy potential.</font></li> <li><font>Extended trigger-reach AR-style grip and 45 reversible safety selector. May be configured with any AR-style grip and selector.</font></li> <li><font>Ruger Precision MSR stock with QD sling attachment points features a bottom Picatinny rail and soft rubber buttpad. The left-folding stock hinge is attached to an AR-style buffer tube and accepts any AR-style stock.&nbsp;</font></li> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img src="http://www.impactguns.com/Data/Default/Images/uploads/ruger/Ruger-precision-rifle.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="134"><img src="http://www.impactguns.com/Data/Default/Images/uploads/ruger/ruger-msr-profile.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="145"><img src="http://www.impactguns.com/Data/Default/Images/uploads/ruger/ruger-msr-takedown.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="188"></p> <p><span><br></span></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><li> <h3>Specifications</h3> </li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Caliber .243 Win</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Cap. 10</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Stock Folding, Adjustable Length of Pull and Comb Height</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Barrel Cold Hammer- Forged, 5R Rifling</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Barrel Length 26.00'</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Folded Length 36.60'</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Overall Length 44.25' - 44.75'</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Height 7.30'</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Width 3.30'</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Weight 11.00 lbs.</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Length of Pull 12.00'- 15.50'</font></li> <li><font style="color: #333333;">Twist 1:7.7"</font></li> <p>&nbsp;</p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="ShippingInfo"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation_ProductAdditionalInformation"><span>This firearm ships to your local gun dealer/gun store (FFL dealer). Use our easy 'FFL SEARCH' in the menu bar at the top of the page. They will gladly provide you with a copy of their license, and charge you a small transaction fee. No Sales Tax will be due (Except in Utah and Idaho).</span><br><br><span>Once we have a copy of their license, we can ship the gun to your local dealer, you then drop by their place, fill out the required paperwork/background check, and take the gun home. We can walk you thru the procedure and help you locate a qualified dealer- just call or email for more information.</span><br><br><span>Our customers generally find this process quite easy and we will help through each step.</span></span></div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <!-- Right Content --> <div class="RightContent" itemprop="offers" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Offer"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_UpdPnlOrderingOptions"> <div class="OrderingOptions"> <div id="Attributes"> </div> <div id="Add-Ons" align="right"> </div> <!--Information : If you change Add-Ons <div> tag ID [EX:<div ID ="Add-Ons">] , then you need to update that name in this javascript [File:"thumbnailviewer.js"] on line no :43 and 111.
